)@@G@@5 ELEMENTS. @E@@@@*.        <DEVICE>  - SAME AS PRINTER, BUT PRINT WILL DJ
)@@G@@BE    @B@@@@*.                    SYMMED TO DEVICE.   @[@@@@*.    @[@@@@DK
)@@G@@*.    @[@@@@*.    @ @@@@*.        PRT  A,B,C,D,E..... @[@@@@*.    @G@@@@DL
)@@G@@*.        OPTIONAL SGS, SPECIFIES THAT THE OUTPUT RUNSTREAM GENERATED   DM
)@@G@@@G@@@@*.        WHEN PROCESSING THE GIVEN ELEMENTS IS TO BE PRINTED BY SDN
)@@G@@SG.   @[@@@@*.    @G@@@@*.        IF THE FIRST ELEMENT IN THE LIST IS 'PDO

)@@G@@LL BE COPIED TO   @A@@@@*.        TAPE2 TO MAKE A BOOTCOPY. @[@@@@*.    DV

)@@G@@            OFF   @[@@@@*.    @E@@@@*.        THIS SGS IS REQUIRED, AND DX

)@@G@@ND WILL MAKE A    @G@@@@*.        TAPE COPY OF ALL THE VOLATILE SYSGEN FEA

)@@G@@          NOT     @^@@@@*.        PACK  NOTHING @#@@@@*.              OKEC
)@@G@@@[@@@@*.    @G@@@@*.        TELLS ENDSYS WHETHER OR NOT TO PACK THE FILEED
)@@G@@S.  THIS CARD IS  @F@@@@*.        OPTIONAL.  IF OMMITTED, ALL THE FILES EE
)@@G@@WILL BE PACKED.   @[@@@@*.    @F@@@@*.        NOT       - RO WILL NOT BEEF
)@@G@@ PACKED.  INSTEAD, IT WILL BE @G@@@@*.                    COPOUT'ED TO AEG

)@@G@@THE FILES.  @G@@@@*.        OK        - (OR ANYTHING ELSE) ALL THE FILESEJ

)@@G@@N  FILE1 <FILE2> <FILE3> ...  @[@@@@*.    @I@@@@*.        THIS SGS IS REEL

)@@G@@@E@@@@          SA,H2     A2,BYTE           . SAVE MORE SCAN INFO @F@@@@VS
)@@G@@          EX        GETC,*A2          . PICK UP THE NEXT CHARACTER@E@@@@VT
)@@G@@          TNE,U     A4,' '            . IS THIS A SPACE     @G@@@@      VU

)@@G@@  A4,077            . IS THIS THE TERMINATOR    @C@@@@          SLJ     VX
)@@G@@  CKLAST            . EOC TEST@E@@@@          TNE       A4,QUOTE        VY
)@@G@@  . IS THIS A QUOTE MARK@H@@@@          J         ENDFB             . ENVZ

)@@G@@RN    @H@@@@/.        SCNREM SUBROUTINE...THIS ROUTINE BEGINS SCANNING FYD

)@@G@@    SCNCOL SUBROUTINE...THIS ROUTINE SCANS FROM THE COLUMN  @F@@@@ .    AE
